Home

Welcome to my home page. Currently, I am working on several small coding projects focused on formalizing theorums and learning Lean. I have also returned as student to Stockholm University and I am finishing a degree in computer science.

I am a vigourously analytic and eccentrically creative person. I have over 7 years working at differentt start up companies in Stockholm, involved in the business and product side. A natural language AI copmany, fintech, governance and regulation ai, and some other smaller companies.

My 2026 new hobby was to pick up bouldering.

Github, only small projects I could make public e.g. a fun C++ "AI" text generator.
